name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted January 8, 2024
msg:We had an amazing staycation at this hotspring resort. I was very impressed with the customer service we recieved. Everyone was incredibly kind and went out of their way to help. The staff has clearly had 5 star training.

 I would like to make particular note of Mr. Lee at the front desk. Upon check-in, he served us and acknowledged that not all the staff spoke English and that we should contact him directly over Wechat if we needed anything. On several occassions I contacted him and he was prompt and curtious. He was a great ambassador for the hotel. For example, room service forgot chicken on on salad, and he promptly pologized and arranged for two new compelmentary salads to be sent (i believe this was an oversight as the hotel was very busy with a special chiristmas dinner that night). 

It is common in Beijing for hotel staff not to speak English, however we did found several memebers of staff that did. For example. when we went to the dining hall, they sent an English speaker over to help us. Further, the dining hall manager checked in with us and personally cleared plates away. Buffet breakfast was above average with western and chinese food. Also, when ordering room service, though they did not speak English, they sent someone to our room with a menu so that we could point to the items we wanted. 

Overall, the hotel is new and to Western standards of cleanliness and quality. Beds and pillows were comfortable. We were with my 2 month old baby and my 85 year old father, all generations enjoyed our time. The hot springs were very clean (not always the case in China) and they were alongside swimming pools with kids climbing apparatice and water ball pit. It was also nice that there were complementary refreshments (snacks and drinks) at the hot springs. In the winter air, the outdoor hotsprings were great. 

Finally., though it wasnt a huge attraction, its nice to see the lammas, chicken and horses. 

Overall, I could not recommend this place more. I will defintely stay again.

It seems there was some electrical problem with the socket. It started to make a spark noise and smelt like burning, so we had to quickly unplug the hairdryer for fear of it going on fire.

The location is in the middle of nowhere, so it's not convenient if you want to buy food or snacks. i personally didn't like the hotel breakfast. It doesn't compare to other international brand hotel standards. 

Overall, it would a pleasant stay, but only because it was suitable for my daughter to swim..

    1. The room. It's quite big. The bathroom is not only separated from wet and dry, but also independent of each partition. The single bed is 1.35 meters, so a two-child family is completely stress-free. Each room has a small balcony which unfortunately cannot be opened. A small suggestion: the night light in the bathroom is too bright.
    2. Catering. The breakfast is quite complete, especially the pancakes on the left side of the door are very good. Of course, overall it's not that impressive. There is a Chinese restaurant on the first floor, which is Sichuan cuisine. The dishes are quite authentic. The pigeons and platters in Cantonese cuisine are a bit salty.
    3. Services. The customer service manager contacted one day in advance, basically meticulous, and the prompts were in place. Epidemic prevention is also very strict, and scanning the code is also indispensable.
    4. Hot springs. It is called Xiyue Hot Spring. There are indoor and outdoor parts, not particularly large, but there is a children's area and a small fish pond, all of which are included in the ticket. The outdoor pool is very comfortable with fewer people. The swimming pool and hot spring are together, not a standard pool, but enough to play. The bathing area is relatively clean, there is a buffet, some snacks and fruits plus pigmented water, it is no problem to have a pad. The little ones can have fun.
    5. Around. There is a picking, which is easy to miss if you want to search for "Diyuan Suihang Agriculture". The tomatoes have been picked by others, and the peppers have been picked a lot. The experience of the little pot friend is very good. A few kilometers to the north, there is an international flower port. There are no flowers and no scenery in winter, but the Butterfly World is okay. It is recommended to buy a package ticket.
    In general, 1-2 nights with family is a good choice.

Based on these requirements, I chose Xinhualian Lijing Hotel. I have only come to eat buffet and hot springs before, and the impression is not bad, this time I will experience the accommodation again.
Due to the late arrival time, I changed my clothes and soaked in the hot spring at 9 o‚Äôclock. The hot spring front desk suggested that the next day should be more abundant. However, because I had an appoin**ent with friends the next day, it is not suitable for children to soak for too long, so I chose Buy a ticket and go in (ticket 168, weekend 218, the same price as in the review, you can pay when you arrive, I heard us discuss changing clothes in the room, and actively asked if the guest is staying in the hotel, and told the guest that the preferential price is 128, so happy üòÉ). Since it was late and there were not many people inside, the children had a great time playing ocean ball in the big pool with lower temperature, and also tried the small pool with special characteristics. Before I left, I went to the beverage area. Although it was approaching the clearing time, the service staff watched us come and asked what to drink. They picked up some smoothies for the children and asked if they could have some snacks. And I opened the hot drink again and asked if I wanted something hot, and the attitude was very good.
The room is also very spacious, the bed is a double bed of 1.35, moderately soft and hard, writing desk, small sofa, coffee table, luggage rack are all complete, the bathroom is also wet and dry partition, there is a bathtub and shower (shower head can be removed and hand held, very suitable Children), the hardware facilities are complete. Room service asked for children‚Äôs bathrobes and slippers. The waiter brought two bathrobes and two pairs of slippers of different sizes for the children to choose from, which was very considerate.
The breakfast on the second day was quite satisfactory. There was no special surprise, but it was basically complete, and everything you wanted was satisfied. It was equipped with children‚Äôs plates and chopsticks.
On the first floor, there are intangible cultural heritage handicrafts, a claw machine, a car to drive (charged items), and a free playroom, which is more suitable for smaller and younger children.

The child‚Äôs family is still very important. During the two-day stay, the manager on duty was very attentive. He delivered fruits, prepared bathrobes for the children, and gave gifts before leaving.
Environmental facilities: We went on a weekend. It took 1 hour from the city to arrive. I don‚Äôt feel that there are too many people (the hot spring is more crowded but acceptable), underground parking is free, the hot spring water is relatively clean, the hotel‚Äôs overall air-conditioning and network environment They are all comfortable. The food and water in the hot spring area are relatively ordinary. The only food is Sachima and Dali Garden buns. The water is basically a blended drink. We only drank lemonade and brought some food for the children. There are many hot spring pools, such as lemon bath, red wine bath, rose bath, mint bath, etc. There are also no outdoor experiences. Children who kiss the fish pond are more interested. In addition, there are 2 playgrounds for children, which are about 38 degrees. The child is hot, about 35 degrees, which is more suitable. You can also swim in a separate area, about 1 meter 2 and the maximum depth is 1 meter 6. You must wear a swimming cap.
The hotel itself has a small children's activity area, which is not too big. It is relatively new for children under 6 years old, and there are many other activities. What we bought is a package, including: intangible cultural heritage experience, alpaca feeding, 5D movies, picking The children are more interested in the intangible cultural heritage experience. The teacher has been encouraging her during the painting for one and a half hours; there are 3 alpacas, the youngest are very popular with most children, and the other two are older and younger. I will be more scared; the 5D movie experience is not so good: it starts at 10 in the morning, but there is no staff at 10 o‚Äôclock. Many children gathered at the door, and the staff came after a long phone call. The picking was outside the hotel. About 2 kilometers, there is no compulsory consumption. Finally, I would like to praise that the breakfast is really good, there are many kinds, each table is accompanied by toys, the children like it, the overall experience is good, and will come again.
